	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Antisemitism</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">For total or partial opposition to <a href="/wiki/Judaism" title="Judaism">Judaism</a> as a religion and <a href="/wiki/Jews" title="Jews">Jews</a> as a religious group, see <a href="/wiki/Anti-Judaism" title="Anti-Judaism">Anti-Judaism</a> and <a href="/wiki/Religious_antisemitism" title="Religious antisemitism">Religious antisemitism</a>.</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>

<li><a href="/wiki/Persecution_of_Jews" title="Persecution of Jews">Judaism</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Religious_antisemitism" title="Religious antisemitism">Religious antisemitism</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-selflink selflink">Antisemitism</a></li>

</tr><tr><td style="padding:0.3em 0.4em 0.3em;font-weight:bold;border-top: 1px solid #aaa; border-bottom: 1px solid #aaa;border-top:1px solid #aaa;border-bottom:1px solid #aaa;">
<a href="/wiki/Portal:Religion" title="Portal:Religion">Religion portal</a></td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:right;font-size:115%;padding-top: 0.6em;"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Religious_freedom" title="Template:Religious freedom"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Religious_freedom" title="Template talk:Religious freedom"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Religious_freedom&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Antisemitism</b> (also spelled <b>anti-semitism</b> or <b>anti-Semitism</b>) is hostility to, prejudice, or discrimination against <a href="/wiki/Jews" title="Jews">Jews</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Oxford_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Oxford-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MWdef_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MWdef-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> A person who holds such positions is called an <b>antisemite</b>. Antisemitism is generally considered to be a form of <a href="/wiki/Racism" title="Racism">racism</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Antisemitism may be manifested in many ways, ranging from expressions of hatred of or discrimination against individual Jews to organized <a href="/wiki/Pogrom" title="Pogrom">pogroms</a> by mobs, state police, or even military attacks on entire Jewish communities. Although the term did not come into common usage until the 19th century, it is now also applied to historic anti-Jewish incidents. Notable instances of <a href="/wiki/Persecution_of_Jews" title="Persecution of Jews">persecution</a> include the <a href="/wiki/Rhineland_massacres" title="Rhineland massacres">Rhineland massacres</a> preceding the <a href="/wiki/First_Crusade" title="First Crusade">First Crusade</a> in 1096, the <a href="/wiki/Edict_of_Expulsion" title="Edict of Expulsion">Edict of Expulsion</a> from England in 1290, the <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Jews_in_Spain#Massacres_and_mass_conversions_of_1391" title="History of the Jews in Spain">massacres of Spanish Jews</a> in 1391, the persecutions of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Inquisition" title="Spanish Inquisition">Spanish Inquisition</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Alhambra_Decree" title="Alhambra Decree">expulsion from Spain</a> in 1492, the <a href="/wiki/Tach_VeTat" class="mw-redirect" title="Tach VeTat">Cossack massacres in Ukraine</a> from 1648 to 1657, various <a href="/wiki/Anti-Jewish_pogroms_in_the_Russian_Empire" class="mw-redirect" title="Anti-Jewish pogroms in the Russian Empire">anti-Jewish pogroms in the Russian Empire</a> between 1821 and 1906, the 1894–1906 <a href="/wiki/Dreyfus_affair" title="Dreyfus affair">Dreyfus affair</a> in France, <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">the Holocaust</a> in <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">German-occupied Europe</a> during <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, <a href="/wiki/Antisemitism_in_the_Soviet_Union" title="Antisemitism in the Soviet Union">Soviet anti-Jewish policies</a>, and Arab and Muslim involvement in the <a href="/wiki/Jewish_exodus_from_Arab_and_Muslim_countries" title="Jewish exodus from Arab and Muslim countries">Jewish exodus from Arab and Muslim countries</a>.
</p><p>The root word <i><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Semite" class="extiw" title="wikt:Semite">Semite</a></i> gives the <a href="/wiki/Misnomer" title="Misnomer">false impression</a> that antisemitism is directed against all <a href="/wiki/Semitic_people" title="Semitic people">Semitic people</a>, <i>e.g.</i>, including <a href="/wiki/Arabs" title="Arabs">Arabs</a> and <a href="/wiki/Assyrian_people" title="Assyrian people">Assyrians</a>. The compound word <i>Antisemitismus</i> ("antisemitism") was first used in print in Germany in 1879<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEBein1990595_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEBein1990595-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> as a scientific-sounding term for <i>Judenhass</i> ("Jew-hatred"),<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTELipstadt201922–25_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTELipstadt201922–25-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEChanes2004150_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEChanes2004150-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTERattansi20074–5_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTERattansi20074–5-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTERoth200330_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTERoth200330-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEJohnston198327_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEJohnston198327-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-laqueur1_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-laqueur1-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> and this has been its common use since then.<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEJohnson1987133_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEJohnson1987133-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTELipstadt201922–25_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTELipstadt201922–25-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-JustJews_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JustJews-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
